In [21]:
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import Dense
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
In [2]:
dataset = np.genfromtxt('FinalBankfraud.csv', delimiter=",", skip_header = True)
In [3]:
#split
X = dataset[:, :-1]
Y = dataset[:, -1]
In [4]:
# Mean normalization
min = X.min(axis = 0) 
max = X.max(axis = 0) 
mean = X.mean(axis = 0)
X = (X - mean) / (max - min)
In [5]:
model1 = Sequential()
# activation functions relu, sigmoid, elu
model1.add(Dense(1, input_dim = len(X[0, :]), activation='sigmoid'))
#model1.add(Dense(1, activation='sigmoid'))
In [6]:
model1.compile(loss='binary_crossentropy', optimizer = 'rmsprop', metrics=['accuracy'])
In [7]:
from sklearn import model_selection
from sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression
test_size = 0.30

X_train, X_test, Y_train, Y_test = model_selection.train_test_split(X, Y, test_size=test_size)

#model1.fit(X_train, Y_train)

#P = model1.predict(X_train)
#accuracy = model1.evaluate(X_train, Y_train)
In [8]:
history1 = model1.fit(X_train, Y_train, validation_data = (X_test, Y_test), epochs= 24)
#epochs should be in 2power = 256, 512, 1024
print(history1.params)

plt.plot(history1.history['accuracy']) # replace with accuracy/MAE
plt.plot(history1.history['val_accuracy']) # replace with val_accuracy, etc.
plt.ylabel('Accuracy')
plt.xlabel('epoch')
plt.legend(['training data', 'validation data'], loc='lower right')
plt.show()

model5 = Sequential()
# activation functions relu, sigmoid, elu
model5.add(Dense(16, input_dim = len(X[0, :]), activation='elu'))

model5.add(Dense(1, activation='sigmoid'))

In [25]:
model7 = Sequential()

model7.add(Dense(32, input_dim = len(X[0, :]), activation='relu'))
#model7.add(Dense(16, activation='relu'))
#model7.add(Dense(8, activation='relu'))
model7.add(Dense(4, activation='relu'))
model7.add(Dense(1, activation='sigmoid'))

model7.compile(loss='binary_crossentropy', optimizer = 'rmsprop', metrics=['accuracy'])

history7 = model7.fit(X_train, Y_train, validation_data = (X_test, Y_test), epochs= 512)
#epochs should be in 2power = 256, 512, 1024
print(history7.params)

plt.plot(history7.history['accuracy']) # replace with accuracy/MAE
plt.plot(history7.history['val_accuracy']) # replace with val_accuracy, etc.
plt.ylabel('Accuracy')
plt.xlabel('epoch')
plt.legend(['training data', 'validation data'], loc='lower right')
plt.show()

In [43]:
model8 = Sequential()

model8.add(Dense(128, input_dim = len(X_test[0, :]), activation = 'relu')) 
model8.add(Dense(64, activation = 'relu'))
model8.add(Dense(16, activation = 'relu'))
model8.add(Dense(8, activation = 'relu'))
model8.add(Dense(4, activation = 'relu'))
model8.add(Dense(1, activation = 'sigmoid'))

# rmsprop, sgd, nadam, adam, gd,
model8.compile(loss='binary_crossentropy', optimizer = 'rmsprop', metrics=['accuracy'])




history8 = model8.fit(X_train, Y_train, validation_data = (X_test, Y_test), epochs= 512)
#epochs should be in 2power = 256, 512, 1024
print(history8.params)

plt.plot(history8.history['accuracy']) # replace with accuracy/MAE
plt.plot(history8.history['val_accuracy']) # replace with val_accuracy, etc.
plt.ylabel('Accuracy')
plt.xlabel('epoch')
plt.legend(['training data', 'validation data'], loc='lower right')
plt.show()

from tensorflow.keras.callbacks import EarlyStopping, ModelCheckpoint
# File name must be in quotes
callback_a = ModelCheckpoint(filepath = "/content/FinalBankfraud.csv", monitor='val_loss', save_best_only = True, save_weights_only = True, verbose = 1)
# The patience value can be 10, 20, 100, etc. depending on when your model starts to overfit
callback_b = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', mode='min', patience= 200, verbose=1)
In [41]:
history = model7.fit(X_train, Y_train, validation_data=(X_test, Y_test), epochs=512, batch_size= 200, callbacks = [callback_a, callback_b])
